# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive analysis of Grafana's plugin signature verification system. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Summary

I've created `/workspace/answer.json` with complete findings on Grafana's plugin signature verification implementation. The system includes:

### Key Components:

1. **Plugin Manifest & Signature Calculation** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go`)
   - `Calculate()` - Orchestrates entire verification process
   - `ReadPluginManifestFromFS()` - Reads signed manifest files
   - `validateManifest()` - Validates manifest structure
   - `Verify()` - Cryptographic signature verification using OpenPGP

2. **Signature Validation** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go`)
   - `ValidateSignature()` - Validates plugin signatures
   - Handles nested plugins and inheritance
   - Enforces signature requirements

3. **Unsigned Plugin Authorization** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go`)
   - `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` - Controls unsigned plugin loading
   - `CanLoadPlugin()` - Checks dev mode and allowlist
   - Prevents unauthorized unsigned plugins

4. **Public Key Management**
   - **Static Keys** (`statickey/static_retriever.go`) - Hardcoded Grafana Labs key
   - **Dynamic Keys** (`keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`) - Downloads from Grafana.com API
   - **KeyStore** (`keystore/keystore.go`) - Caches keys with 10-day sync intervals

5. **Plugin Pipeline Integration**
   - **Bootstrap** - Calculates signature status during plugin creation
   - **Validation** - Validates signatures with `PluginSignatureValidator`
   - **Services Layer** - Records errors for disabled plugins

6. **Configuration** 
   - `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` setting in INI config
   - `PluginsAllowUnsigned` array in `PluginManageme

The plugin ID is in the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` configuration list\\n\\nThis allowlist enforcement prevents unauthorized unsigned plugins while providing a security override mechanism.\\n\\n## Public Key Management\\n\\nPlugin signatures are verified using PGP public keys managed through two systems:\\n\\n**Static Key Retriever** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): Provides a hardcoded Grafana Labs public key for verifying officially signed plugins. The `KeyRetriever` implements the retrieval interface.\\n\\n**Dynamic Key Retriever** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): Downloads and caches public keys from the Grafana.com API. struct validates signatures at the services layer, recording errors with the error tracker for disabled plugins.\\n\\n## Configuration\\n\\nThe unsigned plugin allowlist is configured via:\\n- plugins\\n- `SignatureStatusInvalid`: Failed signature verification\\n- `SignatureStatusModified`: Valid signature but content mismatch\\n- `SignatureStatusUnsigned`: Missing manifest file\\n\\nCorresponding error codes (`ErrorCodeSignatureMissing`, `ErrorCodeSignatureInvalid`, `ErrorCodeSignatureModified`) track signature-related failures for disabled plugin tracking.\\n\\n## signatures\\n- `KeyRetriever`: Retrieves public keys for verification\\n- `KeyStore`: Persists cached public keys\\n- `PluginLoaderAuthorizer`: Authorizes loading unsigned plugins\\n\\n## Wire Integration\\n\\n`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pluginsintegration.go` wires all components together using dependency injection, binding implementations to interfaces and configuring the validation   "text": "Grafana's plugin signature verification system is implemented across multiple files that work together to ensure plugin integrity and security. Here is the comprehensive implementation:\n\n## Signature Manifest and Calculation\n\nThe core signature verification logic resides in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go`. The `Signature` struct implements the `SignatureCalculator` interface and provides the `Calculate()` method which orchestrates the entire verification process. This method:\n1. Checks for a default signature from the plugin source\n2. Reads the plugin manifest from the filesystem using `ReadPluginManifestFromFS()`\n3. Handles unsigned plugins appropriately\n4. Validates manifest structure via `validateManifest()`\n5. Verifies file hashes via `verifyHash()`\n6. Returns a `Signature` struct with the verification result\n\nThe `readPluginManifest()` method decodes PGP-signed manifest files and parses the JSON content. The `validateManifest()` method checks required manifest fields and calls `Verify()` to validate the cryptographic signature using OpenPGP.\n\n## Signature Validation\n\nSignature validation happens in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go` through the `Validation` struct implementing the `Validator` interface. The `ValidateSignature()` method:\n1. Checks if the signature is already valid or internal (core plugin)\n2. Handles nested plugins by inheriting parent signature\n3. Enforces signature requirements based on signature status\n4. Allows unsigned plugins only if authorized via `PluginLoaderAuthorizer`\n5. Returns errors for invalid or modified signatures\n\n## Unsigned Plugin Authorization\n\nThe `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go` file contains the `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` struct implementing `PluginLoaderAuthorizer`. The `CanLoadPlugin()` method allows unsigned plugins if:\n1. They have a valid signature (always permitted)\n2. Grafana is running in development mode\n3. The plugin ID is in the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` configuration list\n\nThis allowlist enforcement prevents unauthorized unsigned plugins while providing a security override mechanism.\n\n## Public Key Management\n\nPlugin signatures are verified using PGP public keys managed through two systems:\n\n**Static Key Retriever** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): Provides a hardcoded Grafana Labs public key for verifying officially signed plugins. The `KeyRetriever` implements the retrieval interface.\n\n**Dynamic Key Retriever** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): Downloads and caches public keys from the Grafana.com API. The `KeyRetriever` struct:\n1. Downloads keys via `downloadKeys()` from `GrafanaComAPIURL/plugins/ci/keys`\n2. Caches keys in the `KeyStore` with configurable sync intervals (10 days)\n3. Implements `GetPublicKey()` to retrieve keys for manifest verification\n4. Supports force-refresh via `PluginForcePublicKeyDownload` configuration\n\nThe `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keystore/keystore.go` provides the `KeyStore` service for persistent caching of public keys using the KVStore infrastructure.\n\n## Plugin Loading Pipeline\n\nSignature verification is integrated into the plugin loading pipeline at multiple stages:\n\n**Bootstrap Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`): The `DefaultConstructor.Construct()` method calls the signature calculator's `Calculate()` method to determine each plugin's signature status before plugin object creation.\n\n**Validation Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go`): The `PluginSignatureValidator` validates signatures via `SignatureValidationStep()`. The `DefaultValidateFuncs()` includes signature validation as a core validation function.\n\n**Services Integration** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go`): The `SignatureValidation` struct validates signatures at the services layer, recording errors with the error tracker for disabled plugins.\n\n## Configuration\n\nThe unsigned plugin allowlist is configured via:\n- `pkg/plugins/config/config.go`: `PluginManagementCfg` struct containing `PluginsAllowUnsigned []string`\n- `pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go`: The `readPluginSettings()` function reads `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` from INI configuration\n\nThis allows administrators to explicitly permit specific unsigned plugins in production while maintaining security by default.\n\n## Signature Status Types\n\n`pkg/plugins/models.go` defines the signature states:\n- `SignatureStatusInternal`: Core plugins bundled with Grafana\n- `SignatureStatusValid`: Successfully verified plugins\n- `SignatureStatusInvalid`: Failed signature verification\n- `SignatureStatusModified`: Valid signature but content mismatch\n- `SignatureStatusUnsigned`: Missing manifest file\n\nCorresponding error codes (`ErrorCodeSignatureMissing`, `ErrorCodeSignatureInvalid`, `ErrorCodeSignatureModified`) track signature-related failures for disabled plugin tracking.\n\n## Interfaces\n\nThe system uses dependency injection with interfaces defined in `pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`:\n- `SignatureCalculator`: Calculates plugin signature state\n- `Validator`: Validates plugin signatures\n- `KeyRetriever`: Retrieves public keys for verification\n- `KeyStore`: Persists cached public keys\n- `PluginLoaderAuthorizer`: Authorizes loading unsigned plugins\n\n## Wire Integration\n\n`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pluginsintegration.go` wires all components together using dependency injection, binding implementations to interfaces and configuring the validation pipeline with signature validation steps.\n\nThis multi-layered architecture ensures plugin integrity through cryptographic verification while allowing administrative overrides for specific use cases."
